<p><b>⇒ <u>17 more</u>:</b> 2. Am Gesteine rauscht die Flut • 3. O die Frauen • 4. Wie des Abends schöne Röte • 5. Die grüne Hopfenranke • 6. Ein kleiner, hübscher Vogel • 7. Wohl schön bewandt war es • 8. Wenn so lindt dein Auge mir • 9. Am Donaustrande • 10. O wie sanft die Quelle • 11. Nein, es ist nicht auszukommen • 12. Schlosser auf, und mache Schlösser • 13. Vögelein durchrauscht die Luft • 14. Sieh, wie ist die Quelle klar • 15. Nachtigall, sie singt so schön • 16. Ein dunkler Schacht ist Liebe • 17. Nicht wandle, mein Licht • 18. Es bebet das Gesträuche
</p>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Liebeslieder Waltzes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Liebeslieder-Walzer&#160;; Love-Song Waltzes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="de, it">Liebeslieder-Walzer</span>; <span title="en, nl">Liebeslieder Walzer, Op. 52</span>; <span title="fr">Liebeslieder</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/181445310">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Liebeslieder_Walzer,_Op._52_(Brahms)">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/181445310">181445310</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Library_of_Congress_Control_Number" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Library of Congress Control Number">LCCN</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://id.loc.gov/authorities/names/n81059979">n81059979</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Integrated_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Integrated Authority File">GND</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://d-nb.info/gnd/300025726">300025726</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Brahms,_Johannes" title="Category:Brahms, Johannes">Brahms, Johannes</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.52
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 48
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td><i>see below</i>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>18 pieces:
<ol><li> Rede, Mädchen, allzu liebes. Im Ländler-Tempo (E major)
</li><li> Am Gesteine rauscht die Flut (A minor)
</li><li> O die Frauen (A major or B-flat major)
</li><li> Wie des Abends schöne Röthe (F major)
</li><li> Die grüne Hopfenranke (A minor)
</li><li> Ein kleiner, hübscher Vogel nahm. Grazioso (A major)
</li><li> Wohl schön bewandt (C minor)
</li><li> Wenn so lind dein Augen mir (A-flat major)
</li><li> Am Donaustrande (E major)
</li><li> O wie sanft die Quelle (G major)
</li><li> Nein, est ist nicht auszukommen (C minor)
</li><li> Schlosser auf, und mache Schlösser (C minor)
</li><li> Vögelein durchrauscht die Luft (A-flat major)
</li><li> Sieh, wie ist die Welle klar (E-flat major)
</li><li> Nachtigall, sie singt so schön (A-flat major)
</li><li> Ein dunkeler Schacht ist Liebe. Lebhaft (F minor)
</li><li> Nicht wandle, mein Licht. Mit Ausdruck (D-flat major)
</li><li> Es bebet das Gesträuche. Lebhaft (B-flat minor)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1869
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1869 (October) - Berlin: <a href="/wiki/N._Simrock" title="N. Simrock">N. Simrock</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Daumer,_Georg_Friedrich" title="Category:Daumer, Georg Friedrich">Georg Friedrich Daumer</a> (1800–1875), after traditional folksongs
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>German
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>
</th>
<td>20 minutes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>voices, piano 4-hands: <span class="expandline">
<dl><dd>soprano, alto, tenor, bass, piano 4-hands (Nos. 1, 2, 5, 6, 8 to 12, 15, 16 and 18)<br />tenor, bass, piano 4-hands (Nos.3 and 14)<br />soprano, alto, piano 4-hands (Nos.4 and 13)<br />soprano or alto, piano 4-hands (No.7)<br />tenor, piano 4-hands (No.17)</span>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>

<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>Version History
<ul><li> Composed for vocal quartet ad lib. and piano 4 hands, 1868–69
</li><li> Arranged for piano 4 hands (without voices) by Brahms, 1874 (first performance in this version: Vienna, 14 November 1874; published in 1874 as "Op.52a"); No.3 exists in two variants. Even the first, 1869, edition allows for performance without voices, however ("voices ad lib.")
</li><li> Arranged for vocal quartet and piano 2 hands by Brahms (first published in 1875)
</li><li> Nos.1, 2, 4, 5, 6, 8, 9 and 11 were arranged for voices with orchestra by Brahms, 1869–70 (first performance in this version: Vienna, 14 November 1874; first published in 1938)
</li></ul>
</td></tr></table>
</div>
